# Shared Blocks

Edit only the `Translation (zh_Hant)` blocks below. `make sync` will propagate
them into every linked shared tree field.

<a id="group-0001"></a>
## Group 0001

- Status: [x]
- References: `2`
- Shared Key: `69999c2c-2710-480e-b8ac-8a8fc6f582e5:text | aee03da5-b399-4274-8db4-fac82c6210d3:text`

<a id="group-0001-blocks"></a>

### Source (en)

~~~text
Although there is no world-wide rule for the application of copyright on data sets (copyright only applies to things that require a so-called "creative step"), it is wise to check for an explicit permission to use a data set and not to assume that data can be used freely just because you can access it. 
Note that copyright laws explicitly *forbid* the use of a copyrighted work, *except* if you get permission. Such a permission is called a "licence". So: if you can not find a licence, you have to assume you can not use the data.
~~~

<a id="group-0001-translation"></a>

### Translation zh-Hant Group 0001

### Translation (zh_Hant)

~~~text
儘管在資料集著作權的適用上並沒有全球一致的規範（著作權僅適用於需要所謂「創作性步驟」的內容），但在使用前，確認資料集是否有明確的使用授權仍是明智之舉，不應因爲資料可以被取得就假設其可自由使用。
請注意著作權法明確「禁止」使用有著作權保護的作品，*除非*您有取得使用權利。如此的使用權被稱為「授權條款（license）」。因此，如果您無法找到授權條款，就必須假定您不能使用該資料。
~~~

### Contexts

  Context: Yes -> What are the conditions of use for this data set -> They are freely available for any use (public domain or CC0) [text]

- [Q] [What are the conditions of use for this database or dataset](<0001 Common DSW Knowledge Model [6f6241d9]/0002 Re-using data [82fd0cce]/0002 Is there any pre-existing data [efc80cc8]/0006 Yes [2663b978]/0001 What existing openly available standard reference data did you... [fcc51962]/0003 Will you be using this reference data set [58401091]/0002 Yes [8a1937d8]/0002 What are the conditions of use for this database or dataset [aee03da5]/translation.md>)

- Status: [x]
- References: `2`
- Shared Key: `df0b2ee3-8e4d-42a1-9bb2-c69228074406:advice | fb96d008-f31a-4a1a-b203-b3f9bb32fcc8:advice`

<a id="group-0007-blocks"></a>

### Source (en)

~~~text
Disadvantage of a general purpose repository is the lack of data-specific features (e.g. 'play' instead of 'download' for an audio file) and limited findability
~~~

<a id="group-0007-translation"></a>

### Translation zh-Hant Group 0007

### Translation (zh_Hant)

~~~text
通用型資料庫的缺點在於，它缺乏專屬於特定資料類型的功能（例如，音訊檔只能播放，無法直接下載），且資料的可查找性有限
~~~
